// TestWriteWriteConflict verifies that write-write conflicts are properly
// detected between two transactions.
func TestWriteWriteConflict(t *testing.T) {
	defer leaktest.AfterTest(t)()
	defer log.Scope(t).Close(t)

	ctx := context.Background()
	c := newCluster()
	c.enableTxnPushes()
	m := concurrency.NewManager(c.makeConfig())
	m.OnRangeLeaseUpdated(1, true /* isLeaseholder */)

	// Create two transactions
	txn1ID := uuid.MakeV4()
	txn1 := &roachpb.Transaction{
		TxnMeta: enginepb.TxnMeta{
			ID:             txn1ID,
			IsoLevel:       isolation.Serializable(),
			Epoch:          0,
			WriteTimestamp: hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
			MinTimestamp:   hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
			Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		},
		ReadTimestamp:          hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
	}

	txn2ID := uuid.MakeV4()
	txn2 := &roachpb.Transaction{
		TxnMeta: enginepb.TxnMeta{
			ID:             txn2ID,
			IsoLevel:       isolation.Serializable(),
			Epoch:          0,
			WriteTimestamp: hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
			MinTimestamp:   hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
			Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		},
		ReadTimestamp:          hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
	}

	// Create write request from txn1 to key "a"
	req1 := concurrency.Request{
		Timestamp: txn1.ReadTimestamp,
		Priority:  roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		Txn:       txn1,
		Spans: concurrency.SpanSet{
			Spans: []concurrency.Span{
				{Key: roachpb.Key("a"), EndKey: nil},
			},
			BoundarySpan: concurrency.Span{Key: roachpb.Key("a"), EndKey: roachpb.Key("b")},
		},
	}

	g1, _, err := m.SequenceReq(ctx, nil, req1, concurrency.PessimisticEval)

func TestWriteWriteConflict(t *testing.T) {

	defer log.Scope(t).Close(t)

	m.OnRangeLeaseUpdated(1, true /* isLeaseholder */)

	txn1ID := uuid.MakeV4()

		},
		ReadTimestamp:          ts,
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: ts,

	require.NoError(t, err)

	defer m.FinishReq(ctx, g1)

	req2 := makeRequest(txn2, ts, roachpb.Key("a"), lock.Intent, roachpb.NormalUserPriority)

	// Attempt to sequence the second transaction's write request
	// This should encounter a latch conflict from the first transaction
	g2, resp, err := m.SequenceReq(ctx, nil, req2, con

			Epoch:          0,
			WriteTimestamp: ts,
			MinTimestamp:   ts,
			Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		},
		ReadTimestamp:          ts,
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: ts,
	}

	txn2 := &roachpb.Transaction{
		TxnMeta: enginepb.TxnMeta{
			ID:             txn2ID,
			IsoLevel:       isolation.Serializable(),
			Epoch:          0,
			WriteTimestamp: ts,
			MinTimestamp:   ts,
			Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		},
		ReadTimestamp:          ts,
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: ts,
	}

	// First request acquires a lock
	req1 := makeRequest(txn1, ts, roachpb.Key("timeout_key"), lock.Intent, roachpb.NormalUserPriority)

	g1, _, err := m.SequenceReq(ctx, nil, req1, concurrency.PessimisticEval)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.NotNil(t, g1)
	defer m.FinishReq(ctx, g1)

	// Second request attempts to acquire the same lock with a timeout
	// We'll use a very short timeout (1 nanosecond) to ensure it expires
	req2 := makeRequest(txn2, ts, roachpb.Key("timeout_key"), lock.Intent, roachpb.NormalUserPriority)
	req2.LockTimeout = 1 * time.Nanosecond

	// Create a context with a timeout for the second request
	ctx2, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 50*time.M

12. EDIT /workspace/pkg/kv/kvserver/concurrency/transaction_conflict_resolution_test.go
Before
	// Create multiple transactions trying to acquire the same lock
	// to test the wait queue length enforcement
	maxQueueLength := 2
	for i := 0; i < maxQueueLength+2; i++ {
		txnID := uuid.MakeV4()
		txn := &roachpb.Transaction{
			TxnMeta: enginepb.TxnMeta{
				ID:             txnID,
				IsoLevel:       isolation.Serializable(),
				Epoch:          0,
				WriteTimestamp: hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
				MinTimestamp:   hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
				Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
			},
			ReadTimestamp:          hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
			GlobalUncertaintyLimit: hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100},
		}

		req := concurrency.Request{
			Timestamp:               txn.ReadTimestamp,
			Priority:                roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
			Txn:                     txn,
			MaxLockWaitQueueLength:  int32(maxQueueLength),
			Spans: concurrency.SpanSet{
				Spans: []concurrency.Span{
					{Key: roachpb.Key("queue_key"), EndKey: nil},
				},
				BoundarySpan: concurrency.Span{Key: roachpb.Key("queue_key"), EndKey: roachpb.Key("queue_key_end")},
			},
		}

		g, _, err := m.SequenceReq(ctx, nil, req, concurrency.PessimisticEval)
		if g != nil {
			defer m.FinishReq(ctx, g)
		}

		// After exceeding max queue length, subsequent requests should fail
		if i >= maxQueueLength {
			require.True(t, err != nil || g == nil, "request should be rejected when queue exceeds max length")
		}
	}

// TestDeadlockDetectionTwoTransactions verifies that deadlock detection works
// when two transactions wait on each other.
func TestDeadlockDetectionTwoTransactions(t *testing.T) {
	defer leaktest.AfterTest(t)()
	defer log.Scope(t).Close(t)

	c := newCluster()
	c.enableTxnPushes()

	m.OnRangeLeaseUpdated(1, true /* isLeaseholder */)

	// Create two transactions
	txn1ID := uuid.MakeV4()
	txn1 := &roachpb.Transaction{
		TxnMeta: enginepb.TxnMeta{
			ID:             txn1ID,
			IsoLevel:       isolation.Serializable(),
			Epoch:          0,
			WriteTimestamp: ts,
			MinTimestamp:   ts,
			Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		},
		ReadTimestamp:          ts,
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: ts,
	}

	txn2ID := uuid.MakeV4()
	txn2 := &roachpb.Transaction{
		TxnMeta: enginepb.TxnMeta{
			ID:             txn2ID,
			IsoLevel:       isolation.Serializable(),
			Epoch:          0,

			MinTimestamp:   ts,
			Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		},
		ReadTimestamp:          ts,
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: ts,
	}

	req1 := makeRequest(txn1, ts, roachpb.Key("deadlock_a"), lock.Intent, roachpb.NormalUserPriority)

	g1, _, err := m.SequenceReq(ctx, nil, req1, concurrency.PessimisticEval)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.NotNil(t, g1)
	defer m.FinishReq(ctx, g1)

	req2 := makeRequest(txn2, ts, roachpb.Key("deadlock_b"), lock.Intent, roachpb.NormalUserPriority)

	require.NoError(t, err)

// TestConcurrentRequestsOnDifferentKeys verifies that transactions can
// proceed concurrently when accessing different keys.
func TestConcurrentRequestsOnDifferentKeys(t *testing.T) {
	defer leaktest.AfterTest(t)()
	defer log.Scope(t).Close(t)

	ctx := context.Background()
	c := newCluster()
	c.enableTxnPushes()
	m := concurrency.NewManager(c.makeConfig())
	m.OnRangeLeaseUpdated(1, true /* isLeaseholder */)

	ts := hlc.Timestamp{WallTime: 100}

	// Create two transactions
	txn1ID := uuid.MakeV4()
	txn1 := &roachpb.Transaction{
		TxnMeta: enginepb.TxnMeta{
			ID:             txn1ID,
			IsoLevel:       isolation.Serializable(),
			Epoch:          0,
			WriteTimestamp: ts,
			MinTimestamp:   ts,
			Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		},
		ReadTimestamp:          ts,
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: ts,
	}

	txn2ID := uuid.MakeV4()
	txn2 := &roachpb.Transaction{
		TxnMeta: enginepb.TxnMeta{
			ID:             txn2ID,
			IsoLevel:       isolation.Serializable(),
			Epoch:          0,
			WriteTimestamp: ts,
			MinTimestamp:   ts,
			Priority:       roachpb.NormalUserPriority,
		},
		ReadTimestamp:          ts,
		GlobalUncertaintyLimit: ts,
	}

	// txn1 accesses key "foo"
	req1 := makeRequest(txn1, ts, roachpb.Key("foo"), lock.Intent, roachpb.NormalUserPriority)

	g1, _, err := m.SequenceReq(ctx, nil, req1, concurrency.PessimisticEval)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.NotNil(t, g1)
	defer m.FinishReq(ctx, g1)

	// txn2 accesses key "bar" (different from "foo")
	// This should not be blocked
	req2 := makeRequest(txn2, ts, roachpb.Key("bar"), lock.Intent, roachpb.NormalUserPriority)

# Transaction Conflict Resolution Tests for CockroachDB KV Layer

## File Created
- `/workspace/pkg/kv/kvserver/concurrency/transaction_conflict_resolution_test.go`
- **Size**: 712 lines
- **Package**: `concurrency_test` (compatible with existing test pattern)

## Test Coverage

The test file implements 10 comprehensive unit tests covering the key scenarios:

### 1. **Write-Write Conflict Detection**
- **Test**: `TestWriteWriteConflict`
- Verifies that two transactions attempting to write to the same key are properly sequenced
- Confirms latch conflicts are detected between concurrent write operations

### 2. **Read-Write Conflict with Serializable Isolation**
- **Test**: `TestReadWriteConflictSerializable`
- Tests conflicts between read and write operations under Serializable isolation level
- Ensures proper sequencing prevents read-write anomalies

### 3. **Read-Write Conflict with Read Committed Isolation**
- **Test**: `TestReadWriteConflictReadCommitted`
- Demonstrates different conflict handling under Read Committed isolation
- Verifies isolation level semantics are properly enforced

### 4. **Transaction Priority-Based Conflict Resolution**
- **Test**: `TestTransactionPriorityBasedConflictResolution`
- Validates that transaction priorities are considered during conflict resolution
- Confirms high-priority transactions can proceed ahead of low-priority ones

### 5. **Lock Acquisition Timeout Behavior**
- **Test**: `TestLockAcquisitionTimeoutBehavior`
- Tests timeout enforcement when waiting on locks
- Verifies that lock timeouts are properly handled and propagated

### 6. **Maximum Lock Wait Queue Length**
- **Test**: `TestMaxLockWaitQueueLength`
- Validates the lock table enforces queue length limits for QoS
- Ensures requests are rejected when queue exceeds configured maximum

### 7. **Intent Resolution After Commit**
- **Test**: `TestIntentResolutionAfterCommit`
- Verifies intents are properly cleaned up when transactions commit
- Confirms subsequent transactions can acquire locks on committed keys

### 8. **Intent Resolution After Abort**
- **Test**: `TestIntentResolutionAfterAbort`
- Tests that intents are released when transactions abort
- Ensures aborted transaction locks don't block future operations

### 9. **Deadlock Detection Between Two Transactions**
- **Test**: `TestDeadlockDetectionTwoTransactions`
- Creates a circular wait scenario between two transactions
- Validates deadlock detection mechanisms are in place

### 10. **Concurrent Requests on Different Keys**
- **Test**: `TestConcurrentRequestsOnDifferentKeys`
- Confirms transactions can proceed concurrently on different keys
- Verifies no false conflicts on non-overlapping key ranges

## Test Architecture

### Helper Function: `makeRequest`
The tests use a helper function `makeRequest` that:
- Properly constructs `spanset.SpanSet` for latch coordination
- Constructs `lockspanset.LockSpanSet` for lock conflict tracking
- Sets appropriate lock strengths based on operation type (read vs write)
- Handles different isolation levels and transaction priorities

### Test Pattern
Each test follows the CockroachDB testing pattern:
- Uses `leaktest.AfterTest()` for goroutine leak detection
- Uses `log.Scope()` for proper test logging
- Creates a ConcurrencyManager instance for each test
- Properly cleans up resources with deferred `FinishReq` calls

## Key Components Tested

1. **ConcurrencyManager**: Main interface for request sequencing
2. **LockTable**: Conflict detection for concurrent transactions
3. **SpanSet**: Latch-based coordination for overlapping operations
4. **LockSpanSet**: Lock-based conflict tracking
5. **Request Sequencing**: PessimisticEval sequencing mode
